Current Commentary

The Abolition of the Indo-Japanese Treaty and Anglo-Japanese Relations 45

(1) Shadows Over the Future of the World Economic Conference

The Washington "fireside chats" have temporarily concluded with the successive returns of the British Prime Minister and the former French Prime Minister. On the surface, the three major powers, Britain, the United States, and France, have reached a considerable understanding on currency issues, tariff wars, trade relations, and war debts, although there are no concrete solutions. The detailed plans have been left for the World Economic Conference in mid-June. Therefore, capitalist economists and the general public are optimistic about this, believing that it can overcome the current economic panic, and there is a possibility of improvement in the new market. However, the fundamental issues of antagonism between Britain and the United States, such as investments in South America, European markets, and Eastern markets, are not discussed, so the actual problems between Britain and the United States still exist in a confrontational form. It is still not eliminated, and how can it be effective to seek consensus through empty words?

Moreover, since the Ottawa Conference of July 21 last year, the British Empire has achieved new unity within itself, from the British mainland to its overseas autonomous territories and colonies. There is a strong tendency to integrate with the British mainland in order to overcome its economic contradictions and break the centrifugal political forces. Apart from the Soviet Union with its special form, France's European alliance is only nominal. The United States has only historical awareness and geographical convenience, but has failed to form a close alliance. The rising Japan, after occupying Manchuria, has been making every effort to link Japan and the Northeast to form its so-called "Japan-Manchuria Economic Alliance" to confront the Soviet Union in the north, control the United States in the east, threaten China in the west, and invade Southeast Asia and India. Therefore, Britain and Japan cannot but be in a position of opposition in economic terms. Although Britain is an advanced capitalist country, its industrial base is mostly in cotton and wool textiles, which is one reason why it cannot be reconciled with Japan. Secondly, British ships sailing overseas mostly carry coal. Many ports from the Strait of Gibraltar to Singapore and Hong Kong do not produce coal. In northern China, Kailuan and Fuzhong, operated with British capital, are the largest, which are opposite to the Japanese Kyushu and Fushun coal mines. This is another reason why Britain and Japan cannot be reconciled. Thirdly, although the areas of British and Japanese investment in China are different, their commercial relations are an irreconcilable struggle. The competition for investment along the Yangtze River is particularly fierce. This is the third reason why the economic interests of Britain and Japan cannot be compromised. However, politically, there are common ground in defending against the Soviet Union, competing with the United States, and suppressing the Chinese national revolutionary movement. Therefore, although the economic opposition between Britain and Japan is becoming more and more acute, the political understanding between Britain and Japan continues. However, economic relations are very important. Take the abolition of the Indo-Japanese Treaty as an example.

(2) The Abolition of the Indo-Japanese Treaty

India is indeed Britain's treasure trove, supplying Britain with raw materials and absorbing a large amount of British investment. However, Britain and India are far apart, and in recent years, the national movement has erupted, and the centrifugal tendency is becoming more and more obvious. Therefore, Japanese goods have taken the opportunity to enter, and the commercial relationship between India and Japan has become closer. Let's list the total value of Japanese goods imported into India in the past two years as follows.

Imports from Japan

1931 110,357,000 Japanese yen 133,165,000 Japanese yen

1932 192,491,000 Japanese yen 116,865,000 Japanese yen

Among them, the import of Japanese cotton cloth into India occupies a major position. The quantity and amount are as follows.

Import Quantity

1931 403,936,000 square yards 49,818,000 Japanese yen

1932 644,458,000 square yards 80,626,000 Japanese yen

The tendency to increase year by year is very obvious. India is the best market for Japan. As for Japan's exports to India (cotton yarn), it is also worth noting. The quantity and amount are as follows.

1931 16,094 bales 5,592,000 Japanese yen

1932 50,836 bales 14,343,000 Japanese yen

The export of Japanese cotton cloth to India is the most promising trade. Last year, the value of cotton cloth alone exceeded 80 million yen. With the addition of cotton yarn, the total value has approached 100 million yen. Now, the Indian government will abolish the Indo-Japanese (Commercial Reciprocity) Treaty on October 10 of this year and implement anti-dumping tariffs. What will be the impact on Japan? The Japanese textile industry has gathered to discuss and plans not to buy Indian cotton in retaliation. However, Japan does not produce raw cotton domestically, and Indian cotton can still find markets in Britain itself, so Japan buying 1.5 to 1.6 million bales of Indian cotton less each year will have a very small impact on India. And India can still seek ways to make up for it in Britain and other places. With the restriction of heavy taxes, cotton cloth and cotton yarn have lost the vast market of India. In this period of deepening economic panic and at the time of active aggression against China, this kind of slow economic blockade is indeed a great blow to Japan.

Although Anglo-Japanese relations are very close politically, economic competition is becoming increasingly fierce. The implementation of increased tariffs in India is only the beginning of the struggle and a preliminary attempt to consolidate the economic alliance within the British Empire. In the future, the struggle between Britain and Japan for the Chinese market may be even more intense than today's tariff war.

World Economic Conference Scheduled to be Held, US Economic Protection Plan Frustrated 46

Economic Conference Preparatory Committee Opposes US Proposal

Roosevelt Begins Negotiations with Various Countries on Reciprocal Trade Agreements

▲National News Agency, London, 29th The World Economic Conference has been decided to be officially convened in London on June 12. At the same time, British Foreign Secretary Simon announced that the British King will personally preside over the opening ceremony. According to reports, a total of 54 countries, including Soviet Russia, will participate in this conference to save the world from the economic disaster. The opening date was agreed upon by British Prime Minister MacDonald and the US President in Washington and was approved by the Organizing Committee meeting today. US President's representative Davis attended the meeting and proposed a gentleman's agreement on a tariff truce. According to the US President's instructions, it was proposed that the invited countries informally agree not to increase tariffs or change import duties from the date of the meeting to the closing of the meeting. However, several representatives opposed this proposal, believing that they could not agree to this truce until the tariff system had been comprehensively reorganized. Therefore, the committee argued that its authority could only prepare for the Economic Conference and had no power to make recommendations to the countries. It was decided only to notify the countries that the United States would propose this truce at the opening of the Economic Conference. Therefore, the US proposal was not included in the Organizing Committee's report.

The US State Department is Quite Disappointed 47

▲National News Agency, Washington, 29th The US State Department was quite disappointed tonight to hear that the US-proposed immediate tariff truce proposal failed to be accepted by the London Economic Conference Organizing Committee. This morning, the US President instructed Davis, the representative stationed in Europe, to submit this proposal. Unexpectedly, although Davis complied with the order, the Organizing Committee believed that it had no power to make recommendations to the countries and could only notify the countries that the United States would propose a tariff truce at the opening of the Economic Conference. As a result, Davis's proposal that no further restrictions should be imposed on trade and the flow of international finance from today onwards failed to be implemented. Tonight, Undersecretary of State Philip stated that the United States made this proposal in the hope of alleviating the fear of further interference in international trade among the world's industrial and commercial sectors, so as to give another boost to increasing business and raising prices. He firmly believes that if there is such a universal agreement, it will be effective immediately. According to reports here, France may accept the truce proposal under certain conditions. Although France agrees to the truce, it is deeply concerned that the international exchange rate will fluctuate sharply before the Economic Conference is convened due to the maintenance of the gold standard, so it has to use tariffs to protect its financial position. Therefore, it hopes to retain some freedom in terms of tariffs.

Five Economic Truce Clauses 48

▲Reuters, London, 29th The World Economic Conference is scheduled to be held on June 12 at the New Geological Museum on South Kensington Street in London, at which time the British Emperor will hold the opening ceremony. This announcement was made by the Economic Conference Preparatory Committee after a meeting at the British Foreign Office today. The preparatory committee was chaired by British Foreign Secretary Simon. US representative Davis stated to the committee that the US representative will propose a tariff truce at the opening of the World Economic Conference, and the proposed clauses will be sent to the invited countries at the same time for prior inspection. According to a detailed view of the US proposal submitted by Davis, the US proposal is not only a tariff truce, but it is more appropriate to call it an economic truce. Its basis is nothing more than advocating that no new obstacles of any kind should be established during the conference to hinder commerce. The US representative will propose at the meeting that there should be no (1) new tariffs, (2) exchange rate restrictions, (3) import and export quotas, (4) prohibitions, and (5) dumping. The duration can be determined by the General Assembly. However, the US government advocates that this truce should remain in effect until the governments of the countries concerned ratify the agreements established by the General Assembly.

Washington Conference Continues 49

▲Reuters, Washington, 29th Discussions on economic events will continue in Washington in the coming week. Representatives from Germany, Italy, Mexico, and Argentina will all gather here next week to discuss events related to the World Economic Conference with President Roosevelt, especially those related to their respective countries.

Negotiations on Reciprocal Trade Agreements Begin 50

▲National News Agency, Washington, 29th A plan will be submitted to Congress next Monday, the content of which will authorize the President to begin negotiations on reciprocal trade treaties. The first country to negotiate with the United States will probably be Canada. Today, US President and Canadian Prime Minister Bennett held a very long meeting and then issued a joint communiqué stating that countries must immediately proceed to raise the level of commodity prices, and said that the talks between the two sides so far have been completely satisfactory.

French Government's Attitude Toward the Truce 51

▲Havas, New York, 29th French representative and former Prime Minister Herriot boarded the "Ile de France" at 2:25 pm today and set sail for France. Herriot stood on the rear staircase and paid tribute to the many well-wishers.

▲Havas, Paris, 29th The French government is extremely pleased with the cordial and frank talks in Washington. If the devaluation of the US dollar does not exceed 15% of the value of hard currency, then France can accept the international compromise on a tariff truce for the sake of public interest. If so, then the issue of repayment of war debts due in December last year and June this year is difficult to regard as a political conclusion before a more general agreement is reached. Moreover, the French side, for the war debts due and to be due, after clarifying the conditions proposed by the US Congress for resolving the war debt issue, may approve the repayment of one installment, but must first be sure that the United States can solve the war debt with a fair method for each debtor country before it can do so.

Japan Considers Countermeasures 52

▲Tokyo, 30th Dispatch from the Japan United Press - The government will hold the final meeting of the six-ministry joint conference at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on May 2nd to decide on Japan's approach to the economic and technical aspects of the Washington Conference. Political issues will not be subject to a definitive policy. The government will issue instructions to its representatives at any time, depending on the attitudes of the various countries at the conference table. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is considering two countermeasures for the Japanese government's approach to the Washington "Little London" Conference: one is to actively advocate, and the other is to respond to the issues raised. The following policies have already been decided internally: A. Japan's active advocacy: (1) Establish the principle of freedom of commerce; (2) Regarding the Far East issue centered on the Manchurian problem, Japan originally opposed the London Conference discussing the Manchurian problem. However, at the Washington Conference, it intends to voluntarily explain the actual situation in the Far East to the new U.S. government, expressing that the current state of (Manchukuo), the many improvements that have occurred before this event, and the establishment of (Manchukuo) are the cornerstones of stabilizing the Far Eastern political situation, etc. It also argues that China's anti-foreign boycott movement has become a constant source of unrest and instability in the Far Eastern market. B. The Japanese government's attitude towards the opponent's claims: (1) The United States advocates the expansion and strengthening of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the United Kingdom and France all agree to this move. If such an agreement is to supplement the Kellogg-Briand Pact, Japan will not actively oppose it, but it must reserve the interpretation of the right of self-defense, which belongs to absolute autonomy; (2) On the issue of unconditional restoration of the gold standard, Japan cannot approve it unless the gold reserve ratio of each country's currency is reduced to an appropriate level; (3) On the reduction of general tariff rates, Japan's tariff system was established earlier than other countries, and its tax rates are also lower than the current tax rates of other countries, so it opposes a uniform reduction by all countries; (4) On the increase and stabilization of silver prices, the United States is a silver-producing country, and the United Kingdom has silver reserves in India. However, Japan not only does not produce silver domestically, but its neighboring countries, such as China, have a silver standard, so it does not want to raise silver prices and would rather stabilize them. An illegal increase in silver prices may seem to increase the purchasing power of silver-using countries on the surface, but in reality, it leads to a rise in the cost of silver production in various countries and chaos in the entire economic sector, so Japan has to be wary of it; (5) However, Japan unconditionally agrees to the adoption of silver as the standard currency to establish a bimetallic standard system.

Our Country and the League of Nations Closely Cooperate 54

The League of Nations Has Repeatedly Sent Experts to China

To Assist in Various Construction Projects

(Geneva) The Chinese government, in accordance with the Technical Cooperation Plan established between China and the League of Nations in 1931, will appoint Mr. Sommerhuel, formerly of the British Ministry of Labor, as an expert for Chinese civil administration agencies, and Mr. Landzh, director of telephone affairs in Frankfurt, Germany, as an expert for Chinese telegraph and telephone agencies. In addition, it plans to appoint several people as experts on postal issues. This cooperation plan also stipulates that China will appoint League of Nations experts to reside in China to serve as liaison between the League of Nations and the National Economic Council of China. In addition, Mr. Lassman, Director of the Health Section of the League of Nations, has also set sail for the East. (Havas Dispatch, 29th)

(Geneva) China has agreed with the League of Nations on a technical cooperation plan and appointed various experts, as reported in another telegram. The details of this matter are as follows: In January 1931, the Chinese government notified the Council of the League of Nations that China had organized the National Economic Council to engage in national construction and hoped to utilize various technical agencies of the League of Nations. The methods of utilization include: the League of Nations sending personnel to reside in China to serve as general liaison between China and the League of Nations; or, in the event of special plans, China requesting the League of Nations to send experts to China to assist; or the League of Nations assisting China in training civil servants; or the League of Nations assisting China in selecting talented experts to help the Chinese government develop education and find ways to facilitate the exchange of knowledge between Chinese and foreign cultural institutions. This cooperation plan of the Chinese government was accepted by the League of Nations in May 1931. The Health Section of the League of Nations has sent several experts to China to conduct temporary research, with a particular focus on medical education. Dr. Borci has been assisting China in organizing health administration and central hospitals for three years. The Cultural Cooperation Section has sent several commissioners to China to investigate educational conditions. After the completion of the investigation, the Chinese side sent several educators to Europe for investigation. The League of Nations also selected three professors to go to Nanjing Central University. The Communications Section of the League of Nations studied methods of flood relief for China, as well as restoring flooded land and reforming the Greater Shanghai port plan. It also sent many engineers to engage in extensive road construction plans. Several thousand kilometers of these roads have been completed. The engineers have also established training schools for Chinese engineers. Regarding financial issues, after Sir Surde contacted the Chinese government, the League of Nations sent financial expert Mr. Quelong to China in February. His mission is for a period of six months. Regarding the flood issue, the League of Nations recommended Sir Simpson to China. After his mission was completed, he returned to Europe. Cooperation between China and the League of Nations involves all issues, so the number of experts sent by the League of Nations is extremely large. It is necessary to appoint another person, in addition to the various experts, to reside in China and serve as liaison. His duty is to report to the Chinese government on how the various technical organizations of the League of Nations can be utilized by the Chinese government. (Havas Dispatch, 29th)

Bulgaria's Sofia is taking stricter precautions. All those suspected of being Communist leaders and organizers, as well as many labor councilors, have been temporarily detained. Communist and Socialist parties in other countries are mostly planning celebrations, and the government is only taking routine precautions and has not issued special orders. However, in several South American countries, due to the large number of unemployed people and the tendency of labor to stir up trouble, the authorities have great power to curb incidents.

▲Tokyo, 30th Dispatch from Reuters - Tomorrow is Labor Day. Laborers of the left and right wings in Tokyo will hold separate parades here to celebrate. The Disarmament Conference Becomes Deadlocked Again 65

Germany Ignores Requests from Britain and France

And Insists on the Principle of Equality in Armaments

▲Geneva, 29th Dispatch from Reuters - Germany's attitude towards the Disarmament Conference and its demand for equality in armaments within a limited period of time have endangered the conference with becoming deadlocked. There is still no progress in this situation today. Chairman Henderson, British representative Eden, and German representative Nadolny met this evening, but still failed to ease the tense atmosphere. It is reported that the German government has reiterated its amendments, ignoring the requests of Britain and France.

▲Geneva, 30th Dispatch from Havas - The Military Quota Committee of the Disarmament Conference will announce on Sunday that certain parts of the German police will be included in the calculation of military quotas. The committee seems to be deciding by a majority vote to include reserve police officers and students in the Disarmament Convention. The same applies to police stationed in barracks, but not to police who do not live in barracks. Chairman Henderson of the Disarmament Conference invited representatives from Britain and Germany in the evening to try to compromise. The German representative, Nadoni, insisted on the various demands made by Germany and refused to budge. People in Geneva are increasingly convinced that the German delegation will not make concessions until the United States, Britain, and France jointly issue a statement next week.

▲Berlin, 30th Dispatch from Havas - A semi-official document commented on the Washington political talks, saying that if the United States abandons its policy of (not participating in any joint action), it will have a significant impact on the work of the Disarmament Conference. If the United States has already given France such assurances, then the German delegation to the Disarmament Conference will have to insist even more on its demands.

▲Berlin, 29th Dispatch from the Guomin News Agency - Today, German Aviation Minister Goering issued a letter to the people of the whole country, advocating the organization of a national aviation salvation association to protect the security of the country and defend against enemy air raids in wartime. Goering said that the countries surrounding Germany all have thousands of bombers, while Germany has almost nothing. The danger is extreme. Therefore, aviation salvation is a matter of vital importance to the German people. To complete the great plan of air defense, it is necessary to unite the people of the whole country and pool their wisdom and strength. This is the main purpose of establishing a national aviation salvation association to awaken the people's attention.

▲Berlin, 29th Dispatch from Havas - Germany's newly built giant aircraft with 2,500 horsepower held a grand naming ceremony today. President Hindenburg personally attended the ceremony. Prime Minister Hitler did not attend because he had to go to Zengcheng. Prussian Prime Minister Goering issued his order on his behalf to name it (Hindenburg). President Hindenburg, accompanied by Deputy Prime Minister Papen and Defense Minister Blomburg, arrived at the Tunberg-Hofer training ground to review the National Defense Forces honor guard. Goering said in his speech that Germany's talent excels in peaceful struggles and surpasses all countries. This is another proof of this.

The Cuban Revolution 66

A Provisional Government is Established in US Territory

Fear and Panic in the Cuban Capital

▲Havana, 29th Dispatch from the Guomin News Agency - Revolutions suddenly broke out in several places in Cuba tonight. It is said that the province of Oriente is actually in the hands of the revolutionary army. At the same time, a well-organized provisional government is waiting in Miami, Florida, in the United States. As soon as it receives a telegram from the revolutionary army in the country, it will immediately return home by plane to command military affairs. As for the government, it is now urgently mobilizing government troops, loading them on wheels, and transporting them to Santiago in hopes of saving the crisis in Oriente Province. At the same time, President Machado has ordered a strict inspection of mail and telegrams. However, according to telegrams received here, the revolutionary organization seems to be widely spread, with Oriente Province as its activity center. This sudden attack on the San Luis military camp, which is an important railway intersection, 40 miles north of Santiago, is said to have destroyed all government military defenses. In addition, many other towns have been occupied. The revolutionary army is now concentrating at its designated location. However, the government, in addition to acknowledging the seriousness of the situation, has not released any other news. Although the capital of Havana appears peaceful, people are in fear and panic. The authorities have sent government troops to defend key points to prevent former President Minocal from landing. It is said that Minocal claimed that as soon as the revolution breaks out, he will immediately return home by plane with his two sons. He also said that the incident in Kemaisuai Province a few days ago was not done by his party, and that the revolution he planned would be a large-scale undertaking. It is also heard that just before the outbreak in Oriente Province, President Machado received a letter requesting him to resign and cede the presidency to a provisional president. Machado ignored it and told his followers that he would definitely not leave office before his term expires next year. It was also heard tonight that the revolutionary organization had rented many empty ships and transported arms and ammunition from foreign ports to small, remote ports in Cuba, secretly unloading them. It is believed that there are no fewer than ten representatives of the former president in the capital of Havana, but the government agencies have not yet been able to detect them.

Britain and India Actively Boycott Japan 71

The Tokyo Asahi Shimbun reported on the 25th that the abrogation of the current Japan-India trade treaty is a major expression of British oppression of Japan. The notice is based on Article 324 of the British Customs Union Act of 1853 (British ships may directly or indirectly prohibit or restrict foreign navigation vessels). If it is implemented, the losses suffered by Japanese ships will be very significant. In the past, the exchange rate between Japanese ships in India, Australia, Australia, Britain, Canada, Britain, and Canada, and Australia has been very favorable. Japanese Troops Reinforce and Attack Nantianmen 74

Japanese Troops at Gubeikou Exceed 30,000

The Reclaiming of Lulong by Commander Weng Zhaoyuan's Division

Special dispatch from Beiping: The Japanese army, withdrawing troops from Luandong, is deploying all its strength to attack Gubeikou, aiming to seize Nantianmen, occupy the high ground, and attack our army from a commanding position. On the 21st, the No. 8 Watchtower suffered a devastating blow, as the watchtower was destroyed by Japanese artillery fire and reduced to powder. However, the Japanese did not succeed. On the morning of the 26th, over 2,000 Japanese and puppet troops crossed the Chao River by wading through the water and launched a fierce attack on the No. 8 Watchtower, Jiepaiyu, and Nantianmen, supported by over ten aircraft and artillery fire, desperately trying to break through. Our troops calmly responded to the attack, with soldiers mostly lying in trenches, using machine guns to sweep the enemy. On the south bank of the Chao River, Japanese corpses piled up like mountains, and the river water turned red. By 4:00 PM, the Japanese had deployed reinforcements and launched another assault. The artillery fire continued incessantly, and the battle became increasingly fierce. Our ambushing troops, taking advantage of their rested state, waited for the enemy's morale to weaken and, at a signal, bravely launched an attack. The enemy was caught off guard and fled towards Chaoshuiguan. Yesterday (the 27th) morning, Japanese aircraft again flew over Nantianmen, Shixiazhen, and other places, dropping bombs. After noon, they launched a fierce artillery attack on Nantianmen. The sound of artillery rumbled throughout the night, but the Japanese still failed to capture it, indicating the intensity of the battle.

The Japanese army is full of schemes, unpredictable and ever-changing. For days, they have been turning the East Railway issue into a serious matter, on one hand, claiming they will use force against Russia and actively increase troops in northern Manchuria; on the other hand, moving their elite troops from Luandong to attack Gubeikou, intending to take the route of Miyun and Shunyi to directly threaten Beiping and Tianjin, annexing North China and completing their so-called "North China State" conspiracy. They have also dispatched another large army to invade eastern Chahar from the Rehe border, adopting a strategy of gradually breaking through our anti-Japanese front, dividing the whole into parts, trying to make our army unable to attend to both the head and the tail, and then driving puppet state rebellious elements to cross the border, thereby concealing their actions from the eyes of the world. Currently, the troops attacking the Gubeikou area include the Pumu, Nishi Yoshiichi, Suzuki, and Kawahara units, totaling over 30,000 men. It is also heard that the Japanese side has a new military plan, deciding to organize future invading armies into smaller detachments to harass separately, instead of concentrated attacks by entire divisions. This move is nothing short of releasing a smokescreen to the international community, further preventing other countries from paying attention, and then acting arbitrarily and doing whatever they want. Therefore, in recent days, troops have continued to be transported from Japan to China, with most heading to northern Manchuria and a small part heading to the various passes of the Great Wall to increase their strength. At present, in the Luandong area, there are also four to five thousand puppet state troops, with one part under the command of Li Jichun and the other part under the command of Zheng Yanhe. Zheng's unit is called the 7th Brigade, but it actually has less than three thousand men and is mostly reorganized from bandits, lacking discipline.

Huang Jie, the Commander Fighting Bravely Against the Enemy at Nantianmen 75

Its organization lacks a unified system, and they are the first to collapse in battle. The Japanese army is forcing this kind of rabble to bear the brunt of the battle, really just using them to eliminate them. This morning (the 28th), according to a certain source, the Japanese army, having repeatedly attacked Gubeikou without making progress, in recent days, in addition to increasing heavy troops continuously arriving for reinforcements, a large amount of supplies and military equipment have been transported from Shenyang to the various passes of the Great Wall. This morning around 5:00 AM, as the sky was just dawning, the Japanese army concentrated artillery fire and continuously attacked our Nantianmen and Daxiaoxinkailing positions. More than forty heavy cannons fired continuously for over five hundred rounds, without stopping for a moment. Smoke filled the air, and the firelight lit up the sky. On the right flank, the Japanese army launched a fierce attack on our position with three infantry columns. Our commander-in-chief, Xu Tingyao, led a large army to the front line to supervise the battle at dawn. All the soldiers fought with a hundred times their usual courage, and a cry of killing shook the valleys. They also dispatched a division of troops to attack the enemy from the rear. The Japanese army, unaware, was in the midst of attacking forward when their lines suddenly became chaotic. Our army attacked from both the front and the rear, cutting off the head and tail of the Japanese army, causing many casualties. The enemy at Nantianmen and the No. 8 Watchtower, under the cover of artillery and aircraft, also attacked us. The battle was exceptionally fierce, and our army responded calmly, but the sacrifices were also extremely heavy.

On the front line of the Beining Railway, Shi Shian's regiment of He Zhuguo's army advanced towards Changli on the 26th. On the night of the 27th, the Japanese army retreated from the east gate, and our army immediately advanced to Changli. On the 28th, the seventh passenger train on the Beining Railway heading east started from Beiping in the morning.

The Commander of the Gubeikou Pass Directs the Battle 76

Although tickets were only sold to Anshan, the passenger train can reach Changli. Telephone and telegraph communications between Qinhuangdao and Tianjin have been restored. The railway authorities have sent workers to repair the tracks on the Qinhuangdao-Changli section, and passenger and freight trains will soon be able to reach Qin Island. Our garrison troops and troops at Beidaihe and other stations are continuing to advance. The Japanese troops retreating from Changli are retreating along the railway line towards Haiyang and other places. Our army may not pursue them relentlessly, but all the troops are still adhering to the principle of resisting any enemy attack, and their morale is very high. As for the reclaiming of Lulong, it is reported that since Li Xingcun's division of Shang Zhen's army reclaimed Qian'an at 9:00 AM on the 23rd, that afternoon, Weng Zhaoyuan's division actively advanced towards Lulong. Weng even took the lead and rode in a car to the Caijiafen area to supervise the troops, and then advanced to Lulong at dusk. The three hundred puppet troops in Lulong City had already fled towards Changli the day before. Moreover, after Lulong was occupied by the Japanese army, they set up their headquarters in the city. Our army once fired artillery shells that hit their kitchen, and after Commander Weng's troops entered the city, they still saw the rubble and scattered tableware. There were many ronin in the Japanese troops. The residents of Lulong City had all fled. During the eight days the Japanese army was in the city, they raped, looted, and massacred on a large scale. Because most of the young women in the city had fled before the city fell, even older women were not spared. It is said that there was an old woman there,

Wounded Soldiers Waiting for Transportation at the Front 77

Who was over sixty years old, was also raped by the Japanese army. There was also a young woman surnamed Tang who could not escape and was gang-raped to death by seven or eight Japanese soldiers. The belongings and money of middle-class families were mostly looted, causing extremely heavy losses. On the 24th, Weng summoned the city's residents and held a mass meeting in the city's parade ground. Weng gave a speech, roughly saying that the army is the people's army, and every citizen is a commander of the army, and all have the responsibility to supervise and urge. Soon, a representative of the people took the stage and spoke, and when he said the phrase "became slaves of a fallen country for eight days," his voice broke with emotion, which shows the high level of public outrage.

Japanese aircraft dropped leaflets on the banks of the Luan River on the 21st, and the language was extremely absurd. Here are a few excerpts to give a general idea: (1) Yellow compatriots, wake up yourselves. Let the people of East Asia govern East Asia. Reflect on yourselves. Destroying China is using barbarians to control barbarians, a vulgar policy of warlords. Looking at history, what did China lose by relying on Europe and America, and what did it gain? The Japanese army's bravery is number one in the world. The Japanese army's weapons are unparalleled in their sophistication. Observations from Shixiazhen - Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng Ya 78

Enemy Aircraft Bombard Everywhere, Turning Towns into Scorched Earth

The Battle at the No. 8 Watchtower Position is the Fiercest

Gubeikou is the only natural barrier that Beiping must pass through to reach Chengde. It has steep mountains and cliffs, naturally dangerous, and the Great Wall winds along its crest. Apart from this pass, there is no other path. Watchtowers are built on the pass, towering majestically in the strategic location. The passage under the tower can only accommodate one car. This is truly a natural barrier that one man can hold against ten thousand. However, the Rehe army abandoned its duty and retreated timidly, making a big mistake. The pass, along with Lengkou and Xifengkou, bid farewell to the motherland of thousands of years and fell under the iron heel of the invaders. As the reporter looked remotely with a mirror at the high ground of a certain defense line to the left and rear of Nantianmen, the form of the natural barrier was clearly visible. Recalling the grand plans of the Qin Emperor and the value of the Great Wall in national defense throughout the generations, I cannot help but feel the contrast between the past and present. The reason why the reporter suddenly recorded this is because it was the third day after leaving Beiping and passing through Sunkouzhen, Niulanshan, Wangjiazhuang, Miyun City, Jiusongling, Chaozhuzhuang, etc., and arriving directly at Shixia, which was also one of the most memorable days of the trip. The first day was a tiring journey, the second day was almost entirely spent in a dungeon where the sun never shone, and the third day was thanks to the kindness of the aircraft (of course, the Royal Army), which gave me a decent opportunity to do some observation and interviews. It was truly a stroke of good luck in misfortune. The day before, after leaving Beiping, a strange fragrance suddenly wafted into the air during the tiring journey. I looked up and saw pear blossoms on the roadside, filling the gardens and valleys, mixed with peach and plum blossoms, like clouds and brocade. The driver said that the place was called Lihua Pit, about fifty or sixty li from Beiping City. The ladies of Beiping City, tired of the urban scenery, often come here to enjoy the fragrance of wild flowers. Before he finished speaking, I caught sight of eight or nine large cars connected end to end, fully loaded with wounded soldiers, stained with blood, lined up on the right side of the road. The pleasure of admiring the pear blossoms was suddenly replaced by an indescribable pain. The national crisis is so severe, yet there are still ladies who are intoxicated in the fragrance of roses. If they were to see the bright red blood blossoms opened by these brave soldiers, I wonder if they would feel the same way. In an instant, the pear blossoms filling the gardens and valleys were no longer visible. The future is uncertain, and the wheels of the car, speeding forward like a whirlwind, I don’t know how many more times they must spin before reaching their destination. This road is slightly flatter than the road to Xifengkou, because that road has more sand, while this road has more dirt, and there are no scattered stones. However, the dust that blinds the eyes and blocks the road is even worse. Along the way, there were many soldiers who could not stand walking and wanted to hitchhike. The drivers all refused sternly. Later, some even tried to grab the front of the car. Only by honking the horn loudly could a bloody path be cleared and we sped away. I suddenly felt a pebble fly past my ear and hit the lower leg of a platoon leader who was snoring loudly against the back wall of the car. It made a loud bang. The platoon leader was in great pain and exclaimed in shock, "Who is it?" A soldier replied, "It's an old villager (a common term for soldiers in the north) who wanted to hitchhike." A certain section chief in a short coat also chimed in, "That's right, it's your armed comrade." Everyone burst into laughter, and the soldier laughed even more uncontrollably. Unexpectedly, the platoon leader, filled with pain and shame, suddenly swung his huge palm and slapped the soldier's cheeks hard. The soldier retaliated with all his might, showering him with fists. The two wrestled into a ball, almost falling out of the car. After being persuaded to stop, one had blood and foam pouring from his mouth, and the other had his oblique robe torn like the Panchen Lama's, but they still glared at each other, wanting to vent their remaining anger. After the battle temporarily ended, the atmosphere in the whole car was silent for a long time. The wheels of the car turned roughly, making them especially loud. The inferior nature of the Chinese people (brave in private fights) can be found anytime, anywhere. It is truly heartbreaking. Arriving at Jiusong Mountain, the car went down a slope. On both sides of the mountains, there are solid

Defensive works. The bank of a river ahead is also densely covered with barbed wire, and deep trenches are dug, enough to overturn enemy tanks and armored vehicles and protect the safety of our anti-Japanese soldiers. A soldier at a certain military station said that this is the third line of defense. Although it is far from the front line, enemy aircraft often come to scout, fearing that they will take advantage of the side roads. Even in Miyun City, which is in the rear, enemy aircraft often come to scout and bomb. On the morning of the 18th, fifteen aircraft flew to the city, soaring in the sky and dropping bombs like rain, about a hundred in total. The whole city was almost a scorched earth. Even the church gospel hall, which hung a foreign flag, was bombed. Fortunately, most of the residents and soldiers took refuge in underground caves, but there were still thirty to forty casualties, and even more livestock had their abdomens torn open and their intestines flowing out, which was extremely tragic. Before he finished speaking, the sound of gongs was suddenly heard in the village. The driver knew that the iron birds were coming and immediately ordered everyone to get out of the car and take cover, and covered the car with green cloth as a talisman. No sooner said than done, the aircraft had already suddenly arrived directly overhead. Fortunately, they did not drop any bombs. After a knowing look, they immediately went their separate ways. When starting the car, the lame platoon leader, who had been mistakenly hit by a stone, arrived late, and needed help getting into the car. But when the aircraft suddenly arrived and everyone quickly took cover, he was like a different person. Although the incident was comical, no one dared to laugh openly, fearing that he would roar again. From here on, the number of troops marching or being transported by car gradually decreased, and they were scattered rather than concentrated. Arriving at Shixia late at night, I got out of the car and visited Mr. Che Qinghe of the Support Association's office, and saw that he was preparing to send a telegram saying "The war situation is unfavorable, and the safety of North China is at stake tonight." I secretly calculated in my heart that if we were to be defeated tonight, what would become of us? Entering the city, there were few people on the road, and most of the shops had their doors bolted shut, with the words "No one inside" written on them. Arriving at the headquarters of the 〇〇 Division, I suddenly heard the phonograph playing "Fourth Son Visits His Mother." A certain adjutant said that this was also a gift for consolation. When the music stopped, Division Commander Huang Jie came out to meet me. After a few words of greeting, he made the following statement, roughly saying that before the 21st, there were only small contacts. Since that day, the enemy has been launching fierce formal attacks on us. The No. 8 Watchtower on the left wing of our Nantianmen defense line was first besieged by the enemy at dawn, with a force of about a thousand. Our stationed troops fought bravely and were all sacrificed under the enemy's fierce artillery fire. The No. 8 Watchtower position was lost. In the evening, a battalion of troops tried hard to counterattack, killing their way to the top of the mountain and recapturing five watchtowers. At dawn on the 22nd, the enemy again sent a machine gun team of five to six hundred men to reinforce, and under the fierce bombing cover of aircraft and artillery, they continued to concentrate their attacks on our No. 8 Watchtower position. Battalion Commander Nie Xin fought bravely and died in battle, and the deputy regimental commander was injured. Subsequently, the deputy battalion commander, company commander, and platoon commander died in battle one after another. Although no one was commanding, the soldiers still fought individually, vowing not to retreat. However, due to excessive casualties, they regained and lost the position. Today, we have counterattacked again, advancing and retreating several times. Both sides have suffered heavy casualties. I was almost shaken by the fact that our artillery fire was not as good as theirs, but fortunately, the morale of our troops was very strong and they responded calmly. In addition, a platoon from our special operations team, which had been missing for two days, returned from outside the pass today and also participated in the battle. With the arrival of other reinforcements at the same time, they managed to hold the line and stabilize it as before. It is the natural duty of soldiers to defend the country. Sometimes, despite exhausting all their strength, they are limited by the situation, and their strength and wishes are contrary. I think the people of the country will be able to forgive them. Public opinion must be fair, and right and wrong must be true. If you encounter the enemy's provocations and malicious slander, do not believe them lightly. At present, there is no way out for the people of the country, especially our soldiers holding guns, except to fight to the death. Fortunately, my soldiers are clearly aware of this due to the pressure of the environment. Currently, our army's ammunition and supplies are still being supplied, and their morale is quite high. However, after this continuous four-day and night battle of sacrifices, if the environment permits, we will have the opportunity to reorganize and replenish. With this profound experience, we will surely be able to achieve even better results in killing the enemy in the future. It was already past nine o'clock when we finished talking, so I said goodbye and left. The whole city was dark and without lights, and the use of flashlights was also limited. I groped along slowly, and the guard at the city gate shouted the password at the slightest sound. Strict vigilance was everywhere. The mountain of the No. 8 Watchtower is twice as high as Nantianmen, and has eight corner towers of the Great Wall, two of which have been destroyed by the enemy. The terrain is extremely dangerous, and it is a place that the enemy must seize and that we must defend. The place was originally only stationed with a company of a certain regiment of Commander Huang's division, which led to the loss due to underestimating the enemy. Although repeated counterattacks were made later, at the cost of the highest sacrifice, it was ultimately of no help, which is a pity. The impact of the lost ground on our army will be discussed later. (April 28th, in Shixiazhen)

Wuhu Abolishes Taels and Adopts Dollars 79

| The Money Industry Agreed to Implement it on May 1st |

Wuhu Dispatch: The money industry here, regarding the issue of abolishing taels and adopting dollars,

After receiving the order from the ministry, they immediately began preparations and held several meetings. After several deliberations, the measures were submitted to various banks for review. Now that Shanghai, Zhenjiang, Yangzhou, and other places have all implemented the measures in order,

Wuhu cannot delay any longer, so they convened another meeting the day before yesterday and discussed it in detail. Everyone said that since these measures have been recognized by the banking industry, they should be implemented on May 1st according to the original plan. Everyone unanimously passed the plan and decided on the following regulations: (1) All current and outstanding silver accounts, as well as various silver notes and contracts, shall be converted to national currency accounts at the rate of 6.785 fen per silver dollar up to April 30th. The standard dollar shall be converted to silver dollar at the fixed price of 7.15 fen. (2) The rice market has always been the largest in Wuhu. When transactions are initiated, the demand for silver is very large. Now, in order to regulate the circulation of the market and finance, the inflow and outflow shall still be settled by remittance, and exchange rates for Shenhan and other places shall be established to meet market supply and demand and to adjust the tightness of cash flow. The cash inflow and outflow shall be subject to the price posted by the association, with an additional five jiao per dollar. The dates for remittance to Shenhan and other places, as well as the procedures for ticket posting and payment, shall remain the same as before. (3) From May 2nd, all current and outstanding national currency accounts shall be converted to remittance dollars at the current market price. (4) All national currency collected and remitted on behalf of others shall be recorded according to the current market price. (5) The interest rate for opening new national currency accounts shall be negotiated separately. (6) Copper coins shall be traded at the market price in units of one thousand copper coins per dollar. (7) If there are any matters not covered in these interim regulations, they may be proposed for amendment at any time. (April 29th)

A Major Fire at the Jinpu Railway Jinan Materials Factory 80

Four Road Timber and Warehouse Buildings Destroyed

Losses Estimated at Around 50,000 to 60,000 Yuan

Jinan Dispatch: The Jinan Materials Factory of the Jinpu Railway, attached to the Dahuaishu Factory in the southwest corner, stores the materials used for train operation between Jinan and Hanzhuang. Last night (the 28th) at 8:00 PM, a fire suddenly broke out. At that time, the southwest wind was very strong, and the fire borrowed the power of the wind.

The momentum became greater and greater, and the firelight could be seen in the city. The factory urgently telegraphed the city to alert the authorities. The Public Security Bureau's fire brigade, the Chamber of Commerce's water association, the Japanese fire brigade, the factory, and the Jinpu Railway's fire brigade rushed to put out the fire. It was not until 11:00 PM that the fire was extinguished. The factory is the only large factory on the Jinpu Railway, with great value and important relations. The loss is estimated at about 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. The details of the fire and rescue are recorded below.

Location of the Fire 81

The materials factory is located in the southwest corner of the factory. In the middle of the factory, there is a pile of discarded road timber, about fifty tons. There is a house northwest of the road timber, containing iron nails. To the west, there is another house containing asbestos. In the iron house to the northeast, there are more than five thousand catties of cotton yarn. In the iron house to the east, there are miscellaneous items such as hemp rope baskets and shoulder poles. The fire initially started on the pile of road timber, and then gradually spread to the surrounding houses due to the strong southwest wind. The fire borrowed the power of the wind, and the wind aided the fire. The firefighters could not get close. The road timber and the above-mentioned four houses were completely destroyed. Although there are no accurate statistics on the losses, they are worth about 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. The material section within the factory is located ten meters away from the fire source, and all the valuable materials are stored there, worth about one million yuan. Further east are the machine factory, iron factory, and the essence of the entire Jinpu Railway, worth tens of millions of yuan. Fortunately, people were sent to protect the surrounding area, and they were not affected.

Rescue Situation 82

When the fire first started, the factory's fire brigade went to the scene with water hoses. The two nearby water pipes were both located on the northeast side of the fire scene. The flames were blown back by the southwest wind, and not only could people not get close, but even water could not be sprayed. Fortunately, four locomotives, No. 13, 16, 38, and 28, were transferred from the station and circled around to the northwest side of the fire scene along the railway to spray water and put out the fire, which began to take effect. On the one hand, people tried their best to carry things out. Hundreds of boxes of gasoline were luckily rescued, otherwise, it would have been unimaginable to add fuel to the fire. It was not until 11:00 PM that the fire was extinguished. At that time, Jinan officials of the Jinpu Railway, such as Engineer Hu Shenghong, Dahuaishu Factory Director Zeng Guangzhi, Qin Wenfan, Materials Factory Director Xu Mingzhi, Jinan Station Director Wang Yuebo, Police Section Chief Liao, and Factory Protection Police Inspector Hu Deyu, all went to the scene to direct the fire fighting. Everyone returned at twelve o'clock, but the factory staff did not rest until four o'clock in the morning. But the embers had not yet completely gone out.

Cause Unknown 83

The cause of the fire has not yet been determined. The factory's one thousand or so workers left work at 5:00 PM and the fire started at 8:00 PM, so it was of course not the workers' fault. However, the coke factory, which is fifty meters southwest of the fire source, burns coke day and night. Every night, the whole place is illuminated like daytime. Moreover, it was a southwest wind that night. It is generally speculated that the embers from the coke factory were blown onto the pile of road timber, causing the fire. The factory has since reported everything to the railway bureau. (April 29th)

Haiyuan Pavilion's Book Collection is Difficult to Sell 84

280,000 Yuan Pledged to a Tianjin Bank Three Years Ago

The Library is Unable to Purchase Due to Excessive Price

Jinan Dispatch: The Haiyuan Pavilion book collection of the Yang family in Liaocheng, with its rare books and exquisite engravings, is world-renowned. The owner, Yang Jingfu, had several contacts with the Shandong Provincial Library, intending to let the library preserve the books through a method of half donation and half sale. Three years of cold and summer passed, but no agreement was reached. Recently, a guest returning from Tianjin talked to the reporter about the Haiyuan Pavilion book collection, saying that the ownership of the books had long been not Yang's, and the inside story was quite important. The following is a record of this: Three years ago, Yang Jingfu failed in business and first sold several Song and Yuan rare books, obtaining a price of 80,000 yuan. To the best of my knowledge, there are the Shicaitang Hanwen Collection and others. Later, as his business became more and more unsuccessful, he exhausted all his possessions and pledged more than ninety kinds of Song and Yuan rare books to a certain bank in Tianjin, obtaining a price of 280,000 yuan. In total, there were more than ninety kinds of books, with a total of 1,120 volumes, with each volume costing 250 yuan. The amount was huge and shocking. The reason why the bank was willing to pay such a high price at the time was that Zhang Xueliang definitely intended to buy it at a price of 400,000 yuan at the time, so it dared to boldly pledge the books. If Yang Jingfu did not redeem it on time, selling it for 400,000 yuan would still give him a profit of 120,000 yuan. Unexpectedly, as soon as the pledge period passed, the September 18th Incident suddenly broke out. Zhang Xueliang, in his frustration, had no time to care about this idle affair, and the previous agreement was put on hold. At that time, Yang Jingfu repeatedly contacted the Lu Provincial Library, but who knew that the ownership was no longer his? The bank had already passed the pledge period and could of course sell it, but the collection included the four classics and four histories of the Northern Song Dynasty, which are unique in the world, were regarded as something that would

Disgrace them, and the asking price was too high, and no one could afford to buy them. After a long time, they could not be sold, and the accumulated capital reached 280,000 yuan, which greatly affected their business. The shareholders expressed their dissatisfaction. Recently, the bank was forced to reduce the price and sell it, stating that they did not want interest and were willing to sell it as long as they received the original 280,000 yuan. At this time, with the current unstable situation and financial panic, no one was willing to buy this non-urgent item with huge funds. Although selling it to foreigners would get a higher price, the export of cultural relics would also violate the regulations. Therefore, as of recently, there is still no solution. The Beiping Library and the Shandong Library both intend to purchase the books, but such a huge amount of money cannot be handled at once, and their efforts are to no avail. According to Haiyuan Pavilion, a famous book collector in China, Wang Xiantang, the director of the Lu Provincial Library, wrote "The Past and Present of the Haiyuan Pavilion Book Collection," which records its origins in detail. Among them, there are more than 500 kinds of rare books from the Song and Yuan dynasties. In recent years, half of them have been destroyed by war and bandits, and the owner of the books, Yang Jingfu, has sold them repeatedly. Only these ninety kinds remain. It is also regrettable that Yang did not keep them. (April 29th)

Wuxi 85

Robbers Successively Rob Two Families

In the county's sixteenth district (Wan'an City), ninety-third ward, Nan Liu Alley, villager Liu Er, a farmer by trade and of modest means, was targeted by over ten robbers wielding pistols late the other night around midnight. They scaled the wall and entered his home, dragging Liu Er from his bed, stripping him of his clothes, and tying him up. They poured cold water into his ears, eyes, nose, and mouth, causing him to nearly die three times. They also confined his daughter-in-law, Ms. Mou, in a room, demanding she reveal the location of hidden silver. They ransacked drawers and chests, stealing sixty-three silver dollars, two leather jackets, and cloth-padded clothing, totaling over two hundred yuan in losses. After obtaining their loot, the robbers headed towards Sima Dun. Not satisfied, they broke into the home of Miao Quanquan, a farmer renting land, in the Sima Dun area. They stole two gold rings and a pair of gold bracelets.

Changzhou 86

Methods for Abolishing the Tael and Adopting the Yuan

The Wu Yi County Chamber of Commerce today (the thirtieth) notified the money changers of the decision to abolish the tael and adopt the yuan with the following methods: (1) Starting May 1st, all existing silver account balances will be converted to yuan at a rate of seven qian and six li per yuan for transfer purposes. (2) All future transactions will follow Wuxi's method of using remittances. Withdrawals in cash will incur a one-day interest fee. (3) Interbank interest rates are not to be included. (5) Business hours are set from 9:00 AM to 6:00 PM.

Thieves Captured at Qishuyan

According to a report by Zhang Xucheng, head of the Wu Yi Qishuyan Security Corps, suspicious individuals were pawning items at the De Yuan Pawnshop in the town. Officers were dispatched to investigate, and the suspects attempted to flee. Wu Xiaokun, Su Jinyuan, and Xie Zhaoxian were apprehended on the spot. Subsequently, another team was sent to nearby Zhujia Village, where Liu Hongde and Shen Tonglang were captured along with clothing, bags, chests, and pawn tickets. Upon interrogation, they confessed to being part of a gang of thirteen, possessing multiple box cannons and pistols. The stolen goods were identified as having been robbed from Di Quanrong's home in Shujia Ba. Liu Haoxi, the town's mayor, turned the five arrested suspects over to the county for interrogation on the 29th.

Yangzhou 87

Bandits in Yangjia Temple Resist Arrest

Bandits have recently been discovered in the Yangjia Temple Cangjie Mountain area bordering the county's 90th and 10th districts. Upon receiving this information, the 10th District Security Corps, led by District Commander Lu, launched a search at 5:00 AM yesterday (the 29th) with over twenty soldiers. Unexpectedly, the bandits resisted arrest. The Security Corps captured a suspect named Jiang Depeng and immediately sent him to the city for detention. A report was also sent to Magistrate Ma, who also served as the county's head of the police, Zhu Xinke to lead dozens of detectives to search. The bandits then opened fire, killing Zhuang Yishan, a patrol officer, with a bullet to the head. Upon receiving this news, Magistrate Ma immediately instructed Chen Xuntao, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, to select capable officers to assist in the suppression. The operation resulted in the death of two bandits and the recovery of two Mauser rifles. In addition, bandit activity has been rampant in the 3rd District. Huang Jinting, the director of the responsible Public Security Bureau, came to the city today (the 29th) to request troops for suppression.

Ningbo 88

Pirates Planning to Rob Dinghai Ship Arrested

Shenjiamen, Dinghai County, is home to the First Patrol Team of the Offshore Water Police Bureau. Shen Ligul, a detective from Taizhou assigned to the team, visited the prostitute A Hong in Lotus Bay on the evening of the 27th around 10:00 PM. There, he encountered five gangsters, including his fellow villager, Chen Liansi. They spoke freely of their shared hometown, unaware that Shen was a detective. Chen and his accomplices confessed that a Dinghai ship would be sailing from Shen to Yong tomorrow, carrying 40,000 yuan in banknotes from the Industrial Bank of China. They had gathered over thirty people, armed with guns, to rob the ship after it set sail. Upon hearing this, Shen remained calm and excused himself. He reported the situation to his team leader, who immediately dispatched a large team of water police to surround the brothel. They arrested Chen and his four accomplices, seizing five Mauser pistols loaded with ammunition. Under interrogation, they confessed to having a pirate ship anchored in the river, with the rest of the gang on board. Team leader Yuan Ti led another team to seize the pirate ship, where they apprehended twelve more gang members, including Xu Laoliu. During questioning, they learned that eight other gang members were still at large and are currently being pursued. The arrested pirates were transferred to the Water Police Bureau for further investigation today.

Citywide Martial Law Declared

According to the National News Agency, the municipal authorities, fearing that counter-revolutionary elements might take advantage of the revolutionary memorial days on May 1st, 3rd, 4th, 5th, 7th, 9th, 18th, and 30th to disrupt public order, instructed the Municipal Public Security Bureau to order all district police stations and teams to be on high alert. Yesterday, Director Wen of the Bureau received a confidential report that someone would be using the public sports ground on Daji Road in the Nanshi district to gather ignorant workers from various factories for a meeting at 1:00 PM today (May 1st Labor Day), posing a potential threat to public order. In addition to instructing Jin Tian, the district chief of the Second District, to increase patrol police around the venue today, Director Wen also ordered Tan Baoshou, the head of the Sixth District in western Shanghai, and Lai Gang and Jin Gong of the Fourth and Fifth Districts in Zhabei to assign multiple armed police officers to guard the entrances of all factories within their jurisdictions. Concurrently, Lu Ying, the head of the detective team, was instructed to order Xia Pinshan, the detective leader in western Shanghai, and Wang Shifu and Xin Jingsheng, the leaders in Zhabei, to coordinate with detectives and plainclothes officers to patrol and supervise the areas starting this morning. Supervisor Gong Xikui dispatched all supervisors and male and female inspectors yesterday to join police officers from various district stations in inspecting pedestrians at key road intersections. Special precautions will be taken today. These personnel will search along Zhonghua Road and Minguo Road, near the boundaries of the foreign concessions, and arrest any suspicious individuals. Personnel have also been dispatched to guard and protect the north and south railway stations and telephone bureaus to prevent any incidents. Over twenty police squad cars will patrol the city to assist. Message to Workers

The City General Labor Union issued a message to all workers in the city for the May 1st commemoration, stating: "Dearest workers of the city, today is the great and enthusiastic International Labor Day, celebrating the victory of European and American workers over capitalists. On May 1, 1886, tens of thousands of workers in Chicago, USA, held a tragic and grand demonstration demanding an eight-hour workday, eight hours of rest, and eight hours of education, breaking away from the previous abuse of endless labor. This movement eventually achieved victory, and workers in various parts of Europe and America made similar demands on this day, achieving similar victories, and designated May 1st as International Labor Day every year. This is something that we should all celebrate. Today, as we commemorate Labor Day amidst the serious national crisis, and the precarious situation, and celebrate the victory of workers in various countries of the world, we must recognize the following: (1) The reason why European and American workers were able to achieve the eight-hour system is because they had a conscious will and united solidarity. The grand demonstration on May 1, 1886, was an expression of their spirit of sacrifice and struggle. Although they were under the oppression of the military force of capitalist politics at that time, they resolutely carried out this enthusiastic and great movement, finally shattering the dreams of the capitalists and achieving final victory. Therefore, when we commemorate May 1st, we should emulate the fearless spirit of struggle of European and American workers, unite and break the aggression of international capitalism, resist the unreasonable oppression of domestic capitalists, and strive for a human life. (2) China is a country with backward production. Various industries and commerce cannot compete with foreign countries. Recently, due to the fierce competition from foreign goods, domestic products have been severely hit. For example, the recent reduction in working hours by Chinese-owned yarn factories due to sluggish sales is affected by the dumping of Japanese yarn. If this continues, Chinese industry will be on the verge of bankruptcy, and the livelihoods of our workers will inevitably be desperate. Therefore, under this situation, we must emulate the hardworking and dedicated spirit of European and American workers, improve production, improve skills, reduce the cost of production, and improve the quality to compete with foreign goods, save the endangered Chinese industry, and achieve our own true benefits. (3) Since September 18th, the lost territories in the Northeast have not been recovered, and Yu and Re have successively fallen. Recently, Tianjin and Beijing are in danger, and North China is shaken. The tragedy of national subjugation is imminent. Workers in the entire city should share the difficulties of the times, strive for sincere cooperation between labor and capital, eliminate all disputes between labor and capital, intensify the work of resisting Japan, and vigorously promote the boycott of Japanese goods, jointly saving this serious national crisis. Otherwise, if the country is destroyed and our families are broken, what benefits can we get? What eight-hour system can we demand? The above three points are what the Union wants to tell all workers in the city on this May 1st commemoration. We hope that our dearest workers will work hard and move forward, break through all the current difficulties, and achieve our final victory.

Soviet Ambassador to China, Bogomoletz, has decided to visit Chairman Lin of the National Government tomorrow morning to present his credentials. The reporter was received by the Chinese Counselor, Oshanin, who stated the following:

Departing for Capital This Morning 91

Oshanin said, "The date for the presentation of credentials has been confirmed. Ambassador Bogomoletz, along with his wife, my wife and I, Counselor Bykov, Deputy Consul-General Milikiewicz stationed in Shanghai, and Chief Secretary of the Embassy, Kesin, a total of seven people, will take the 9:25 AM express train from Shanghai to Beijing this morning (the 1st). Permanently Stationed in Capital 92

The Ambassador has decided to be permanently stationed in the capital to discuss all diplomatic issues between China and Russia. However, whether he will stay in Beijing after presenting his credentials or return to Shanghai will depend on the situation after arriving in Beijing. New Consul General to Arrive 94

The new Consul General and consuls in Tianjin and other places will be formally decided after Ambassador Bogomoletz presents his credentials. They will then come to China from Vladivostok with their secretaries to take office.

Treaty Issues 95

Regarding your (addressing the reporter) inquiry about China and Russia negotiating a treaty of friendship and a non-aggression treaty, according to international practice, no political or commercial issues should be discussed before the presentation of credentials. Therefore, I am not in a position to comment. After Ambassador Bogomoletz visits Chairman Lin and presents his credentials, if there are any such issues, I will do my best to release information.

Wang's Recovery: Premier Wang suffered from carbuncle, and his condition is good after being treated by doctors during his previous visit to Shanghai. The wound is gradually healing, but it is very slow. Chu himself is scheduled to return to Beijing last night.

National Goods Groups Oppose Municipal Council's Factory Inspection 98

Petition Submitted to the Municipal Government Yesterday Requesting Negotiations Based on Reason

All National Goods Factories Vow to be the Backbone

The Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association and the Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association submitted a petition to the Municipal Government yesterday, protesting the Municipal Council's seizure of the right to inspect factories. The original text is as follows: "Petition regarding the Public Concession Municipal Council seizing the right to inspect factories, destroying the production of national goods, requesting strict negotiations based on reason to protect national rights. Factory inspection is an important task for social production, and the Factory Inspection Law is the entire law of our country. Now, the Public Concession Municipal Council, based on the tax amount of a minority of taxpayers and the resolution of the Westerners' meeting, has revised the annex to the Yangjingbang Regulations, seizing the right to inspect factories and issue factory licenses. If implemented, it will not only infringe on sovereignty and violate laws, but also restrict the freedom of Chinese citizens to operate businesses and limit the establishment of factories, destroying the production of national goods and implementing a new economic aggression policy. The cunningness of their methods and the malice of their intentions are unbearable. This matter concerns the interests of the national goods industry and is of great importance. As groups of national goods factories responsible for protecting interests, we issued a serious declaration in the newspapers yesterday, resolutely opposing it, in order to awaken the attention of citizens. We also convened a factory representative meeting a few days ago and unanimously expressed opposition, vowing to be the government's backbone. It was resolved on the spot to (1) petition the Municipal Government to negotiate strictly and protect national rights; (2) send letters to national goods groups to send personnel to organize a committee against the Municipal Council's seizure of the right to inspect factories, concentrating the strength of the protest. In addition to sending letters to the groups to organize regular meetings, we hereby submit a petition to the Municipal Government for serious negotiations and arguments based on reason in order to protect national rights and benefit national goods. Our association leads all national goods factories and vows to be a strong backbone. We anxiously await your orders."

To Continue Sending Special Envoys to Assist Huang Xuanwei

Qian Tong Cables Executive Yuan Offering Suggestions

Regarding the turmoil in Xinjiang, the Central Government has appointed Huang Musong to go there to express condolences and investigate the truth in order to completely resolve the dispute.
