Spring and Autumn

Maintaining Property 211

— Zhan Lu

Maintaining property, what kind of term is that? If you interpret it literally and think it refers to midwives waiting for childbirth, then you would be completely mistaken.

But look, in the occupation section of various forms, apart from filling in farmer, worker, merchant, soldier, politician, and academic, many people fill in the words "maintaining property". This refers to guarding the inheritance of one's ancestors, being the young master who never runs out of things to eat and use, which is also considered a very bright and upright occupation.

Coincidentally, in the mother's teachings of the Ming Dynasty's Wen clan, it says: (How can children and grandchildren rely solely on their ancestors to live? Heaven creates a person, and naturally provides for their food and clothing. If they are willing to take on various occupations, big and small, they will naturally achieve results. Nowadays, seeing the children of various families, with long sleeves and large shirts, eating and drinking in comfort, their parents love them and dare not mention labor. Even if their ancestors left millions in assets, they will inevitably be trapped in poverty!) Unexpectedly, the family precepts of a 17th-century old lady still hold true today. "Providing for one's food and clothing" is the inherent duty of everyone. Relying on one's ancestors to live is already shameful. What's more, to be arrogant and disregard everything, carrying the signboard of a young master, and claiming to be "maintaining property" in society, I'm afraid this kind of occupation is not very bright and upright.

What old Mrs. Wen said: (Long sleeves, big shirts, eating and drinking in comfort) is still the habit of 17th-century young masters. Nowadays, not counting rampant prostitution and gambling, smoking a few pipes of opium, marrying a few concubines, and being hawked by antique ghosts selling (fake Tiger Hill) antiques and dubious calligraphy and paintings are already considered stable members of the property-maintaining class. Others, unspeakable, unspeakable!

This kind of property-maintaining, in the 17th-century era, already had the danger of what old Mrs. Wen said: (Inevitably being trapped in poverty). (Because the way of today does not change the customs of today), can it be included only by the words (trapped in poverty)? Young masters, wake up.

(Note) Wen Huang of the Ming Dynasty, originally named Yi Jie, described his mother's education and wrote the book "Wen's Mother's Teachings". Only a few excerpts are found in Chengshi's compilation, and the complete book has not been seen.

Preface to (May First) 212

— Hua Ling

Today is (May First), also known as (Labor Day). This day is usually full of events, so I predict that tomorrow's newspapers will have several news items that are both ordinary and extraordinary. I (am good at observing the color of the sky and predicting good and bad fortune,) and now I write a few predictions below. Whether they are accurate or not, let's wait for tomorrow's breakdown. (The following is the main text of the prediction)

May 1, 1933, Moscow held a grand labor day memorial ceremony, followed by a parade with 100,000 participants. All Soviet Union countries stopped working to hold commemorations.

A special martial law in the city of Berlin, the Brownshirts mobilized the whole team, and suppressed the riot. Obstacles spread through the streets, so as to hinder the parade. At noon, a small squad of Communists gathered to protest in a certain place, throwing bricks and glass bottles into the windows of a certain building. The Brownshirts rushed to the news, and a conflict broke out, resulting in casualties on both sides. In the evening, there were still small conflicts in several places.

Italy is on high alert, the country is calm, and workers work as usual.

Although there are rallies in France, the emotions are indifferent.

The capital of Spain, Madrid, and all over the country, held enthusiastic celebrations, and there were small conflicts with the royal party in the evening. Three Catholic churches were destroyed.

London detectives were mobilized to strictly prevent demonstrations by unemployed workers and famine groups. However, apart from a few groups holding memorial meetings, the city was calm. The parliament discussed the issue of unemployment relief.

American veterans planned to gather in Washington to petition, but it did not happen. Workers across the country took a holiday, and the streets of various cities were full of drunkards.

There were disturbances everywhere in Japan, especially in Tokyo, where the military and police were very active. As a result, more than 170 people were arrested, and a professor and a celebrity were also arrested.

In Shanghai, reactionary elements planned to sabotage a certain construction project, but the conspiracy failed due to strict precautions. In the afternoon, in Nanjing Road and Xiaoshadu, there were several small groups of students and workers shouting reactionary slogans and distributing leaflets, and two suspected youths were arrested. Reactionary slogans were found on electric poles in the Xiahui Road area. The Chinese area was calm in the evening. Curfew was imposed early.

Women as Commodities 213

— Bai Ju Er

Women are like a commodity. Before marriage, they are kept by their parents, and their bodies must not be tainted or damaged, so that those who ask for her in the future may enjoy it well. Once married, she belongs to her husband, who can toss her around, whip her, and drive her as he pleases. If he likes her, he can use her as a tool for sexual gratification. If he dislikes her, he can abandon her and treat her as dead stock. When she is widowed, respectable families consider her an ominous object and confine her to her room until she dies. Poor families treat her as unsold stock and hurriedly look for a buyer to sell her off cheaply.

A woman raised in a poor family in the countryside is like a gold ingot. When she grows up, the money from selling her body can be used for her younger brother's wedding expenses, for her parents' funeral expenses, or even to pay off debts.

A woman who marries a poor husband is like an ox with a ring through its nose, beaten to death, worked to death, starved to death... only to stop when she is buried.

A woman raised in a wealthy family in the city is like a darling, a money tree, and a pearl in the palm of her parents. To her elder brothers and sisters-in-law, she is like a thorn in their side, a money-losing commodity, and a burden outside the bamboo fence.

A woman who marries a wealthy husband is like a useless person who must ride in a carriage even to walk a few steps. She must call a servant even to take an object, relying on electric fans when it's hot and stoves when it's cold.

Alas, sisters! To treat a living person like dead stock is intolerable, utterly intolerable!

Nightingale Sequence 214

— Fei Tie

Sweet Springs glow with torchlight, boiling the waters of Sanggan. Northern geese arrive, inquiring about the past, delicate gauze restrains plum blossoms. Hear tell of thunderbolts flying mid-air, children laughing, saying heavenly flowers fall. Pointing to the imperial city tombs, barbarian horn cannot stir thoughts of return. First news of east wind, shaking the door, moving the window, bitterly casting off the wandering son. Distant longing urges onward, geese arrive but the person does not. Abandoning Zhuyai, strategic plans tacitly agreed, weigh the scales, cease labored calculations. Fearing dawdling, crossroads wandering, other thoughts arise. Deep, silent rests the harbor, drunken dance, revelry, yet easily startles from drowsy slumber. Machine grinding, relying on unstable ramparts, sweeping across wind and rain. Flesh confronts edge, pillow on spear, swallow tears. Requests for aid cut off, Jing Sha bustling at night, dried fish begging for a single drop from the West River, allowing courier carts to tail spin, in pained exhaustion. Welcoming the Big Dipper, guests, teaching each person to ascend the hall, what is being said in the Springs and Autumns, lies. The rise and fall carries responsibility, a widow from Lu, also casts off red and green silks. Now comes news, the shoulders and backs of Youyan, overlook the Qin cities, horses drinking dry the sources, nesting crows rise. Calling to heaven, no way, panicked battles and guards, deep ulcer, extending to the lungs, fearing the Yangtze River's natural barrier is difficult to rely on in the end. Heartbroken, not a visitor, night chants, should cry long songs, tears fill the paper.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 215

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 5: Brewing Tea to Pass the Long Night, Mourning the End of the Year, Raising High the Slogan of Resisting Tyranny

He laughed: I heard that he also has a daughter, why isn't she here? Zhao Ziqiang laughed: Our old brother here, can't forget women no matter what. Tian Qing said: Isn't life just the three major elements of clothing, food, and housing, and then women? Old man Zhao laughed and came out, saying: Company Commander Tian, what else are you not satisfied with? I heard that you have a good female student friend in the city, why are you talking about other women? Tian Qing laughed: Oh! Unbelievable, the old man can also say such jokes. Zhao Ziqiang took out his iron-cased watch to take a look, and laughed: Let's go into the city first, come back to my place for lunch later, it's only half a day's leave, don't spend it muddleheadedly. Tian Qing said: We just sat down, are we leaving? Yin Deren laughed: You are a bit insincere, clearly wanting to fly into the city, don't you want to leave right away? Everyone laughed and walked out the door, just in time for the long-distance bus, and it only took more than twenty minutes to enter Xizhimen. Zhao Ziqiang said: Brother Guan's house, is Xiao Tian going? I don't think you need to go, just send a message to your sister-in-law to say hello, that's enough. Tian Qing put his hand to his forehead and laughed: When you get to Brother Guan's place, don't joke around anymore, as soon as you mention him getting married, our Brother Guan will object. Going is a must, coming to the city specifically to pay New Year's greetings, how can there be no reason not to go? Zhao Ziqiang said: Joking is playing. I also want to say a fair word. Brother Guan is tired enough of wives and children, and his head hurts as soon as you bring it up. In fact, who can be like him, having such a large group of children? Tian Qing pulled on his coat hem and laughed: With our second brother's words, I am going to desperately attack the path of love again. The three of them were talking on the street when they heard a loud crash that echoed for a long time. Yin Deren tilted his head to listen and said: What's that? Such a loud noise. Zhao Ziqiang said: What don't you understand, it's the student lords shouting slogans again. As he spoke, he saw white paper fluttering in the air, and a dark crowd of heads crowded forward under the white light. Zhao Ziqiang pulled the two of them, retreated a few steps to the side of the street, letting this gust of wind pass. At the very front, there were twenty or thirty unarmed policemen, followed by three big students, one holding a megaphone, two holding large bamboo poles, with a white cloth stretched across both sides, with words as big as copper basins written on it: "Recover the Northeast! Down with the Japanese Consortium!" (58)

Love and Traps 217

A girl with newly awakened knowledge, especially a beautiful modern miss, steps into the society of independent living.

When she first meets men, it seems that they all have a gentle and considerate attitude, and their sweet and touching words can strike a chord in people's hearts.

A beautiful face, a handsome suit, adept at games, sports, and dancing, and with a pleasant demeanor that makes people happy to see.

(Flirting and seduction) are completely manipulated in the hands of others! After getting to know each other, she can't bear to leave him for a moment, and he keeps sending her intoxicating love letters, often asking her to be with him! Dancing, watching movies, he tries his best to stir up the girl's emotions, from friendship to love, and practices consensual love.

But what is the result? Men have never been sincere and heartfelt (to grow old together)!

He only has a momentary interest, he is a man who plays with romance, a youth who is fickle, and he envies you for your beautiful face!

Finally, he abandons her out of coldness and heartbreak!

One wrong step leads to eternal regret!

It seems that women are more infatuated. Once they meet a soulmate boyfriend, they think of the dream of a honeymoon.

They believe it without a doubt, but men are always using cunning tricks!

Dating is not as simple as ideal, and making boyfriends is especially a dangerous thing.

(Carefully and cautiously) society's traps are laid out in front of individuals

Home Gardening Work 218

— Juan Yun

The weather is sunny, and all things are flourishing. The azure sky, the lush green leaves, and the vibrant flowers add infinite interest to people's lives.

Even with just a small plot, or even a few feet of empty space in front of the steps, planting some touching flowers is worthwhile. One doesn't need ("a pot of wine among the flowers, drinking alone with no one to share"). Just taking a stroll in front of the flowers in your spare time can bring a deep sense of enjoyment.

Since ancient times, beautiful women have especially cherished flowers as if they were their lives! It seems that flowers can evoke a great deal of empathy in women.

If you are preparing to improve a lonely and desolate home, now is the time. Quickly engage in home gardening work. Here are a few small research notes on gardening that can be used for reference:

Planting flowers and scattering seeds must follow a certain order. The soil should not be too dry, nor should it be too wet. If the weather is too dry, or if it hasn't rained for many days, remember to loosen the soil to allow it to absorb some moisture.

Seeds should be sown in rotation throughout the four seasons, so that beautiful flowers can be seen throughout the year.

American Women and Japanese Women 219

— Miao Shen

Some people say that women's rights are very developed in America. However, it is more accurate to say that American women receive special treatment in society. This is because American women do not have much equality in politics and economics (it can be said to be relative equality). However, in social situations, women receive special deference from men in general. For example, a husband treats his wife as if she were a deity. When going out together, the husband will help his wife put on her shoes, drape her coat over her shoulders, and open doors for her, while he follows behind. If his wife has something to carry, he will carry it for her. Wives generally consider this to be natural and show no gratitude. Therefore, some people say that American husbands are slaves.

The women with the lowest status in the world, and who also consider themselves to be the most inferior, are the Japanese. Japanese women are as docile as sheep. A husband's words are not only commands but are practically imperial decrees! No matter how bad a husband is, the wife should not criticize his shortcomings, as it would harm her virtue. The husband can beat and scold his wife at will. When the husband returns home, the wife must, as a matter of course, kneel to greet him. (Kneeling is the most respectful greeting in Japan.) Therefore, some people say that Japanese husbands are tyrants.

Talk

Reverse Argument 220

— Tian Fang

Good articles are often found in the opposite, so-called between the lines. If you look at it from the front, you are the number one fool. Those who know how to write articles will not do this, and those who know how to read articles will not be fooled.

Speaking of writing articles, we have no shortage of this kind of skilled technique. This skill becomes even more humorous when applied to actions, but few people understand it.

We can learn how to make soy sauce from the methods of brewing wine. Similarly, extremely vulgar and unbearable words can be hit from behind extremely glorious articles, because if you don't say it, I'm still a little unclear. Once you say it, I understand even better, the so-called (trying to cover up only makes things more conspicuous). Like blowing soap bubbles, the blower only sees its size, but the onlookers can easily see the emptiness inside, and the collapse is not far away. This is also a meaning of drawing inferences and can resolve stubbornness.

For example, if a corrupt merchant is caught here, everyone righteously rises up and says (execute him)! This is certainly a well-deserved death, but all the officials, gentry, ladies, and patrons who directly or indirectly created this corrupt merchant are all pardoned. However, the degree and quantity of evil done by these people are no less than that of the corrupt merchant. So, when one is executed, a second one rises. Underneath every corrupt merchant, there are countless similar corrupt merchants hidden.

Furthermore, as prominently reported in the newspapers, there was (saving the country with beautiful faces) and later (saving the country with dancing), with enthusiastic participation and emotional listeners, which was extremely popular for a time. So the reporter also kept writing (received so many love letters today), (so many tickets sold), and as a result, there were people carrying weapons and money to buy fried rice. A piece of mutton attracts all the mosquitoes and ants. Human's inferior nature, once it involves wealth and lust, cannot be concealed in the slightest. As a result, the titles of (patriotic woman) (national salvation dance queen) are highly elevated, but we cannot imagine what is underneath them?

Looking through the newspaper reports, there are also news such as big swords killing enemies, thirteen-year-old children joining the army, eighty-year-old men committing suicide out of concern for the country, and donating two military vehicles to the volunteer army, etc. These are all happy events, but where are our airplanes and cannons? Where are the military vehicles? What kind of situation is flashing behind these headlines! Please, readers, think carefully!

A Night of Luxury 221

— Kuang Bei

About half a month ago, late one night, or perhaps in the early morning, suddenly a series of (pa-pa-pa) firecracker sounds came from outside, like a Japanese machine gun raining down during the January 28th Incident, and it happened to be in the same area—Baoshan Road XX Lane. This made me feel in my blurred sleep as if I was watching two scenes being shown simultaneously. Fortunately, the January 28th Incident had long passed, and many new, unconnected Western-style houses had been built on Baoshan Road. Although the Japanese machine guns were turning towards North China and firing rapidly, Shanghai could still sing a song of (universal peace).

The next morning, I got up and went outside the lane to make tea. On my way back, I noticed these big characters on the right-hand wall at the entrance of the lane: (XX Residence Celebrates a Happy Occasion - Enter Here). This suddenly reminded me of the firecracker sounds from last night. After all, they were for someone else, so I didn't have the leisure to investigate and see which number XX Residence was or to what extent they were celebrating their happiness. I just hurried back to my own residence.

During the day, the lane was still as quiet as usual, except for the morning toilet ritual around 7 or 8 o'clock and the noisy hustle of vegetable vendors around 9 or 10 o'clock. Besides that, there was no significant urgent news.

As dusk approached, a knock suddenly came from outside. After a moment, the sub-landlord came in to discuss with me: (The XX Residence at XX number is celebrating a happy occasion. They just sent two representatives to invite me to attend. May I ask if you will send a gift, sir?)

He kept repeating (It's a big shot!) (It's a big shot!) I didn't pay attention to anything else, but (big shot) (big shot) kept spinning in my mind.

After nightfall, the situation in the lane was completely different. Needless to say, the sounds of drums, shouts, and laughter blended into one, coming in waves. Even outside my window, there were frequent hurried footsteps. I couldn't resist walking out the door. Ah, I saw that at the end of the lane, people's heads were packed together like swaying wheat ears, and the brightly lit gasoline lamps emitted a dazzling white light. Ah, the happy occasion was there, but there was no way to squeeze in. I truly felt a sense of (impassable) resentment. I looked up at some of the windows on the left and right, and they were all packed with people, and I couldn't climb up anymore. (Good, one more!) Was it a magic trick, a Kunqu opera, or something else? I couldn't say for sure. Suddenly, four brand-new limousines with bright electric lights drove into the lane. Naturally, the four people sitting in them were celestial-like dancers with (jade legs and soft breasts). Sure enough, I heard a shout: (The dancing star has arrived!) This made me anxious, but being anxious was useless. I walked back, disappointed. Then the sub-landlord also walked back, disappointed, saying: (It was really beautiful to watch, but there were too many people, so I couldn't see it properly!)

The next day, I went out and made a special detour in front of the XX Residence. A bucket-sized gate lantern on the threshold was still emitting a gray-yellow light. The lane at the entrance was scattered with all kinds of paper scraps, fruit peels, and exploded firecracker debris. Unfortunately, the main door was tightly closed, and I had no way to see the luxurious interior. From then on, whenever I went in and out, I always made a detour around the XX Residence. Yes.
